1602  SET_BIT(RCC->APB2ENR, RCC_APB2ENR_LTDCEN);\
1603  /* Delay after an RCC peripheral clock enabling */ \
1604  tmpreg = READ_BIT(RCC->APB2ENR, RCC_APB2ENR_LTDCEN);\
1605  UNUSED(tmpreg); \
1606  } while(0U)

5737 /*------------------------------- PLL Configuration --------------------------*/
5738 #if defined(STM32F410Tx) || defined(STM32F410Cx) || defined(STM32F410Rx) || defined(STM32F446xx) ||\
5739  defined(STM32F469xx) || defined(STM32F479xx) || defined(STM32F412Zx) || defined(STM32F412Vx) || \
5740  defined(STM32F412Rx) || defined(STM32F412Cx) || defined(STM32F413xx) || defined(STM32F423xx)
5741 
5774 #define __HAL_RCC_PLL_CONFIG(__RCC_PLLSource__, __PLLM__, __PLLN__, __PLLP__, __PLLQ__,__PLLR__) \
5775  (RCC->PLLCFGR = ((__RCC_PLLSource__) | (__PLLM__) | \
5776  ((__PLLN__) << RCC_PLLCFGR_PLLN_Pos) | \
5777  ((((__PLLP__) >> 1U) -1U) << RCC_PLLCFGR_PLLP_Pos) | \
5778  ((__PLLQ__) << RCC_PLLCFGR_PLLQ_Pos) | \
5779  ((__PLLR__) << RCC_PLLCFGR_PLLR_Pos)))
5780 #else
5781 
5810 #define __HAL_RCC_PLL_CONFIG(__RCC_PLLSource__, __PLLM__, __PLLN__, __PLLP__, __PLLQ__) \
5811  (RCC->PLLCFGR = (0x20000000U | (__RCC_PLLSource__) | (__PLLM__)| \
5812  ((__PLLN__) << RCC_PLLCFGR_PLLN_Pos) | \
5813  ((((__PLLP__) >> 1U) -1U) << RCC_PLLCFGR_PLLP_Pos) | \
5814  ((__PLLQ__) << RCC_PLLCFGR_PLLQ_Pos)))
5815  #endif /* STM32F410xx || STM32F446xx || STM32F469xx || STM32F479xx || STM32F412Zx || STM32F412Vx || STM32F412Rx || STM32F412Cx */
5816 /*----------------------------------------------------------------------------*/

5818 /*----------------------------PLLI2S Configuration ---------------------------*/
5819 #if defined(STM32F405xx) || defined(STM32F415xx) || defined(STM32F407xx) || defined(STM32F417xx) || \
5820  defined(STM32F427xx) || defined(STM32F437xx) || defined(STM32F429xx) || defined(STM32F439xx) || \
5821  defined(STM32F401xC) || defined(STM32F401xE) || defined(STM32F411xE) || defined(STM32F446xx) || \
5822  defined(STM32F469xx) || defined(STM32F479xx) || defined(STM32F412Zx) || defined(STM32F412Vx) || \
5823  defined(STM32F412Rx) || defined(STM32F412Cx) || defined(STM32F413xx) || defined(STM32F423xx)
5824 
5828 #define __HAL_RCC_PLLI2S_ENABLE() (*(__IO uint32_t *) RCC_CR_PLLI2SON_BB = ENABLE)
5829 #define __HAL_RCC_PLLI2S_DISABLE() (*(__IO uint32_t *) RCC_CR_PLLI2SON_BB = DISABLE)
5830 
5831 #endif /* STM32F405xx || STM32F415xx || STM32F407xx || STM32F417xx || STM32F427xx || STM32F437xx || STM32F429xx || STM32F439xx ||
5832  STM32F401xC || STM32F401xE || STM32F411xE || STM32F446xx || STM32F469xx || STM32F479xx || STM32F412Zx || STM32F412Vx ||
5833  STM32F412Rx || STM32F412Cx */
5834 #if defined(STM32F446xx)
5835 
5862 #define __HAL_RCC_PLLI2S_CONFIG(__PLLI2SM__, __PLLI2SN__, __PLLI2SP__, __PLLI2SQ__, __PLLI2SR__) \
5863  (RCC->PLLI2SCFGR = ((__PLLI2SM__) |\
5864  ((__PLLI2SN__) << RCC_PLLI2SCFGR_PLLI2SN_Pos) |\
5865  ((((__PLLI2SP__) >> 1U) -1U) << RCC_PLLI2SCFGR_PLLI2SP_Pos) |\
5866  ((__PLLI2SQ__) << RCC_PLLI2SCFGR_PLLI2SQ_Pos) |\
5867  ((__PLLI2SR__) << RCC_PLLI2SCFGR_PLLI2SR_Pos)))
